<script type="text/plain" data-service="youtube" data-category="marketing" id="external-link-icon-js-after">
function externalLinkIcon() {

    var icon = '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 20 20">' +
               '<path d="M9 3h8v8l-2-1V6.92l-5.6 5.59l-1.41-1.41L14.08 5H10zm3 12v-3l2-2v7H3V6h8L9 8H5v7h7z" fill="currentColor"/></svg>';

    var container = document.querySelector('.entry-content');
    if (!container) return;

    var links = container.querySelectorAll('a');

    var socialDomains = [
        'facebook.com', 'twitter.com', 'linkedin.com', 'pinterest.com',
        'instagram.com', 'youtube.com', 't.me', 'whatsapp.com'
    ];

    links.forEach(function(link) {

        // Conditions d’exclusion
        if (
            !link.href ||
            link.host === window.location.host ||
            link.href.startsWith('tel:') ||
            link.href.startsWith('mailto:') ||
            link.href.startsWith('#') ||
            socialDomains.some(domain => link.href.includes(domain)) ||
            link.classList.contains('external-icon-added')
        ) {
            return;
        }

        // Ajouter l’icône
        link.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', ' ' + icon);
        link.classList.add('external-icon-added');

        // Bonnes pratiques sécurité
        link.setAttribute('rel', 'noopener noreferrer');
    });
}

window.addEventListener('load', externalLinkIcon);

//# sourceURL=external-link-icon-js-after
</script>

<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">OOPS !</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;">Je suis désolé, le lien ne semble pas fonctionner. </span></p>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-999999-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color wp-elements-1b6416ae2cf91130d969efd1a72c3249" style="background-color:#331509">J'ai besoin de votre soutien !</h3>



<div class="wp-block-group has-999999-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color wp-elements-f37c7239c8112417ebb3c4f3a18a1ec4" style="background-color:#331509"><div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
<div style="height:6px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>

Merci pour votre soutien.</p>

	<option class="level-0" value="146">Visites Guidées&nbsp;&nbsp;(8)</option>
	<option class="level-0" value="148">Visites Insolites&nbsp;&nbsp;(12)</option>
</select>
</form><script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
( ( dropdownId ) => {
	const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
	function onSelectChange() {
		setTimeout( () => {
			if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
				return;
			}
			if ( dropdown.value && parseInt( dropdown.value ) > 0 && dropdown instanceof HTMLSelectElement ) {
				dropdown.parentElement.submit();
			}
		}, 250 );
	}
	function onKeyUp( event ) {
		if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
			dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
		} else {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
	}
	function onClick() {
		delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
	}
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
	dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
})( "cat" );

//# sourceURL=WP_Widget_Categories%3A%3Awidget
</script>
